I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
MudSelect does not scroll to selected item on open
### Before reporting

- [x] I searched existing issues
- [x] I tried in private/incognito browser

### What went wrong?

MudSelect does not scroll to selected item on open because Items are populated after OpenMenu() due to component lifecycle.

What happens?
When opening a MudSelect that already has a selected value, the dropdown does not scroll to the selected item. Instead, it always shows the top of the list.

Root Cause
In versions 9.x, the registration mechanism for MudSelectItem was refactored. Items now register with the parent MudSelect via MudSelectContext during the render phase (OnAfterRender). However, the OpenMenu() method, which contains the scroll logic, is called earlier — in response to a user click.

At the moment OpenMenu() executes, the Items collection is still empty because the child MudSelectItem components have not yet registered. Consequently, the condition index > 0 fails, and no scrolling occurs.

### Reproduction link

https://try.mudblazor.com/snippet/cYwUaeQuHUYrHOnF

### Reproduction steps

1. Create a MudSelect with several MudSelectItem components.
2. Select any item that is not the first in the list.
3. Close and reopen the select dropdown.
4. The dropdown shows the top of the list without scrolling to the selected item.


### Version (bug)

v9.0.3

### Version (working)

v8.15.0

### Environment

Chrome

### Blazor rendering mode

WASM

</pr_description>

    15	    /// <summary>

    17	    /// </summary>
    18	    /// <typeparam name="T">The kind of object being selected.</typeparam>
    19	    /// <seealso cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/>
    20	    /// <seealso cref="MudAutocomplete{T}"/>
    21	    public partial class MudSelect<T> : MudBaseInput<T>, IMudSelect, IMudShadowSelect
    22	    {
    23	        private string? _activeItemId;
    24	        private bool? _selectAllChecked;
    25	        private string? _multiSelectionText;

    47	        public MudSelect()
    48	        {
    49	            _context = new MudSelectContext<T>(this);
    50	            Adornment = Adornment.End;
    51	            IconSize = Size.Medium;
    52	            using var registerScope = CreateRegisterScope();
    53	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(MultiSelection))
    54	                .WithParameter(() => MultiSelection)
    55	                .WithChangeHandler(() => UpdateTextPropertyAsync(false));
    56	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<IEqualityComparer<T?>?>(nameof(Comparer))
    57	                .WithParameter(() => Comparer)
    58	                .WithChangeHandler(OnComparerChangedAsync);
    59	            _openState = registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(Open))
    60	                .WithParameter(() => Open)
    61	                .WithEventCallback(() => OpenChanged);
    62	            _selectedValuesState = registerScope.RegisterParameter<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>?>(nameof(SelectedValues))
    63	                .WithParameter(() => SelectedValues)
    64	                .WithEventCallback(() => SelectedValuesChanged)
    65	                .WithChangeHandler(OnSelectedValuesChangedAsync)
    66	                .WithComparer(() => new SequenceComparer<T?>(Comparer));
    67	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(FitContent))
    68	                .WithParameter(() => FitContent)
    69	                .WithChangeHandler(OnFitContentChanged);
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        protected string OuterClassname =>
    73	            new CssBuilder("mud-select")
    74	                .AddClass("mud-width-full", FullWidth)
    75	                .AddClass("mud-width-content", FitContent && !FullWidth)
    76	                .AddClass(OuterClass)
    77	                .Build();
    78	
    79	        protected string Classname =>
    80	            new CssBuilder("mud-select")
    81	                .AddClass(Class)
    82	                .Build();
    83	
    84	        protected string InputClassname =>
    85	            new CssBuilder("mud-select-input")
    86	                .AddClass("mud-readonly", GetReadOnlyState())
    87	                .AddClass(InputClass)
    88	                .Build();
    89	
    90	        protected string FillerClassname =>
    91	            new CssBuilder("mud-select-filler")
    92	                .AddClass("d-inline-block")
    93	                .AddClass("invisible")
    94	                .AddClass("mx-2", Variant == Variant.Text)
    95	                .AddClass("mx-4", Variant != Variant.Text)
    96	                .Build();

   470	        /// <summary>
   471	        /// Whether the <c>Value</c> can be found in the list of <see cref="Items"/>.
   472	        /// </summary>
   473	        /// <remarks>
   474	        /// When <c>false</c>, the <c>Value</c> will be displayed as a string.
   475	        /// </remarks>
   476	        protected bool CanRenderValue
   477	        {
   478	            get
   479	            {
   480	                if (MultiSelection)
   481	                {
   482	                    return false;
   483	                }
   484	
   485	                if (ToStringFunc is not null && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(ToStringFunc(ReadValue)))
   486	                {
   487	                    return false;
   488	                }
   489	
   490	                if (!_context.TryGetShadowItemByValue(ReadValue, out var item))
   491	                {
   492	                    return false;
   493	                }
   494	
   495	                return item.ChildContent != null;
   496	            }
   497	        }
   498	
   499	        protected bool IsValueInList => _context.TryGetShadowItemByValue(ReadValue, out _);
   500	
   501	        /// <summary>
   502	        /// Builds fallback accessibility attributes for the focused select trigger.
   503	        /// </summary>
   504	        /// <remarks>
   505	        /// <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> keeps focus on its trigger while the popup is open, so the trigger publishes the combobox relationship to the popup list.
   506	        /// </remarks>
   507	        private Dictionary<string, object?> GetInputUserAttributes()
   508	        {
   509	            var attributes = new Dictionary<string, object?>(UserAttributes, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
   510	            attributes.TryAdd("role", "combobox");
   511	            attributes.TryAdd("aria-autocomplete", "none");
   512	            attributes.TryAdd("aria-controls", _listboxId);
   513	            attributes.TryAdd("aria-expanded", _openState.Value ? "true" : "false");
   514	            attributes.TryAdd("aria-haspopup", "listbox");
   515	
   516	            if (!attributes.ContainsKey("aria-label") && !attributes.ContainsKey("aria-labelledby") && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label))
   517	            {
   518	                attributes["aria-label"] = Label;
   519	            }
   520	
   521	            if (_openState.Value && _activeItemId is not null)
   522	            {
   523	                attributes.TryAdd("aria-activedescendant", _activeItemId);
   524	            }
   525	
   526	            return attributes;
   527	        }
   528	
   529	        /// <summary>
   530	        /// Builds the attributes applied to the internal popup list.
   531	        /// </summary>
   532	        /// <remarks>
   533	        /// Provides the stable list identifier and list-level semantics owned by <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>.
   534	        /// </remarks>
   535	        private Dictionary<string, object?> GetListUserAttributes()
   536	        {
   537	            var attributes = new Dictionary<string, object?>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
   538	            {
   539	                ["id"] = _listboxId
   540	            };
   541	
   542	            if (MultiSelection)
   543	            {
   544	                attributes["aria-multiselectable"] = "true";
   545	            }
   546	
   547	            return attributes;
   548	        }

   550	        /// <summary>
   551	        /// The icon to display whether all, none, or some items are selected.
   552	        /// </summary>
   553	        /// <remarks>
   554	        /// Only applies when <see cref="MultiSelection"/> is <c>true</c>.
   555	        /// If all items are selected, <see cref="CheckedIcon"/> is returned.
   556	        /// If no items are selected, <see cref="UncheckedIcon"/> is returned.
   557	        /// Otherwise, <see cref="IndeterminateIcon"/> is returned.
   558	        /// </remarks>
   559	        protected string SelectAllCheckBoxIcon
   560	        {
   561	            get
   562	            {
   563	                if (!_selectAllChecked.HasValue)
   564	                {
   565	                    return IndeterminateIcon;
   566	                }
   567	
   568	                return _selectAllChecked.Value ? CheckedIcon : UncheckedIcon;
   569	            }
   570	        }
   571	
   572	        /// <summary>
   573	        /// Selects the item at the specified index.
   574	        /// </summary>
   575	        /// <param name="index">The ordinal of the item to select (starting at <c>0</c>).  When <see cref="MultiSelection"/> is <c>true</c>, the item will be added to the selected items.</param>
   576	        public async Task SelectOption(int index)
   577	        {
   578	            if (index < 0 || index >= Items.Count)
   579	            {
   580	                if (!MultiSelection)
   581	                {
   582	                    await CloseMenu();
   583	                }
   584	
   585	                return;
   586	            }
   587	
   588	            await SelectOption(Items[index].Value);
   589	        }
   590	
   591	        /// <summary>
   592	        /// Selects the item with the specified value.
   593	        /// </summary>
   594	        /// <param name="value">The value to select.  When <see cref="MultiSelection"/> is <c>true</c>, the selection is cleared if it was already selected.</param>
   595	        public async Task SelectOption(T? value)
   596	        {
   597	            var comparer = Comparer ?? EqualityComparer<T?>.Default;
   598	
   599	            if (MultiSelection)
   600	            {
   601	                // Toggle selection
   602	                if (!_selectedValues.Add(value))
   603	                {
   604	                    _selectedValues.Remove(value);
   605	                }
   606	
   607	                var converted = _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet).ToList();
   608	                var text = string.Join(Delimiter, converted);
   609	
   610	                if (MultiSelectionTextFunc is not null)
   611	                {
   612	                    await SetCustomizedTextAsync(
   613	                        text,
   614	                        selectedConvertedValues: converted,
   615	                        multiSelectionTextFunc: MultiSelectionTextFunc
   616	                    );
   617	                }
   618	                else
   619	                {
   620	                    await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(text, updateValue: false);
   621	                }
   622	
   623	                UpdateSelectAllChecked();
   624	                await BeginValidateAsync();
   625	            }
   626	            else
   627	            {
   628	                // Highlight before closing
   629	                await HighlightItemForValueAsync(value);
   630	
   631	                await CloseMenu(false);
   632	
   633	                // Early exit if unchanged
   634	                if (comparer.Equals(ReadValue, value))
   635	                {
   636	                    await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync(comparer);
   637	                    return;
   638	                }
   639	
   640	                // Replace selection
   641	                _selectedValues.Clear();
   642	                _selectedValues.Add(value);
   643	
   644	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value);
   645	                _elementReference.SetText(ReadText).CatchAndLog();
   646	            }
   647	
   648	            if (MultiSelection)
   649	            {
   650	                await HighlightItemForValueAsync(value);
   651	            }
   652	
   653	            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync(comparer);
   654	
   655	            FieldChanged(_selectedValues);
   656	
   657	            if (MultiSelection && typeof(T) == typeof(string))
   658	            {
   659	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync((T?)(object?)ReadText, updateText: false);
   660	            }
   661	
   662	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   663	        }
   664	
   665	        /// <summary>
   666	        /// Opens or closes the drop-down menu.
   667	        /// </summary>
   668	        /// <remarks>
   669	        /// Has no effect if <c>Disabled</c> or <c>ReadOnly</c> is <c>true</c>.
   670	        /// </remarks>
   671	        public async Task ToggleMenu()
   672	        {
   673	            if (GetDisabledState() || GetReadOnlyState())
   674	            {
   675	                return;
   676	            }
   677	
   678	            if (_openState.Value)
   679	            {
   680	                await CloseMenu(true);
   681	            }
   682	            else
   683	            {
   684	                await OpenMenu();
   685	            }
   686	        }
   687	
   688	        /// <summary>
   689	        /// Opens the drop-down menu.
   690	        /// </summary>
   691	        /// <remarks>
   692	        /// Has no effect if <c>Disabled</c> or <c>ReadOnly</c> is <c>true</c>.
   693	        /// </remarks>
   694	        public async Task OpenMenu()
   695	        {
   696	            if (GetDisabledState() || GetReadOnlyState())
   697	            {
   698	                return;
   699	            }
   700	
   701	            await _openState.SetValueAsync(true);
   702	            _needsHighlightAfterRender = true;
   703	            UpdateIcon();
   704	            StateHasChanged();
   705	
   706	            //Scroll the active item on each opening
   707	            if (_activeItemId != null)
   708	            {
   709	                var index = Items.FindIndex(x => x.ItemId == _activeItemId);
   710	                if (index > 0)
   711	                {
   712	                    var item = Items[index];
   713	                    await ScrollToItemAsync(item);
   714	                }
   715	            }
   716	
   717	            //disable escape propagation: if selectmenu is open, only the select popover should close and underlying components should not handle escape key
   718	            await KeyInterceptorService.UpdateKeyAsync(ElementId, new("Escape", stopDown: "key+none"));
   719	        }
   720	
   721	        /// <summary>
   722	        /// Closes the drop-down menu.
   723	        /// </summary>
   724	        /// <remarks>
   725	        /// Has no effect if <c>Disabled</c> or <c>ReadOnly</c> is <c>true</c>.
   726	        /// </remarks>
   727	        public async Task CloseMenu(bool focusAgain = true)
   728	        {
   729	            await _openState.SetValueAsync(false);
   730	            UpdateIcon();
   731	            if (focusAgain)
   732	            {
   733	                StateHasChanged();
   734	                await OnBlur.InvokeAsync(new FocusEventArgs());
   735	                _elementReference.FocusAsync().CatchAndLog(ignoreExceptions: true);
   736	                StateHasChanged();
   737	            }
   738	
   739	            //enable escape propagation: the select popover was closed, now underlying components are allowed to handle escape key
   740	            await KeyInterceptorService.UpdateKeyAsync(ElementId, new("Escape", stopDown: "none"));
   741	        }
   742	
   743	        /// <summary>
   744	        /// Clears all selections.
   745	        /// </summary>
   746	        /// <remarks>
   747	        /// To reset validation errors (e.g. required), use <see cref="ResetValueAsync"/>
   748	        /// </remarks>
   749	        public async Task ClearAsync()
   750	        {
   751	            await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(default, false);
   752	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(null, false);
   753	            _selectedValues.Clear();
   754	            await BeginValidateAsync();
   755	            StateHasChanged();
   756	            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync();
   757	            FieldChanged(_selectedValues);
   758	        }

   794	        private async Task OnComparerChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<IEqualityComparer<T?>?> arg)
   795	        {
   796	            // Apply comparer and refresh selected values
   797	            _selectedValues = new HashSet<T?>(_selectedValues, arg.Value);
   798	            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync(arg.Value);
   799	        }
   800	
   801	        private async Task OnSelectedValuesChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>?> arg)
   802	        {
   803	            var value = arg.Value;
   804	
   805	            // Update internal HashSet with new values - make a defensive copy to avoid shared references
   806	            // The HashSet uses the Comparer for equality checks and ensures uniqueness
   807	            _selectedValues = value != null ? new HashSet<T?>(value, Comparer) : new HashSet<T?>(Comparer);
   808	
   809	            // Notify all subscribed items of the selection change
   810	            await _context.NotifySelectionChangedAsync();
   811	
   812	            if (!MultiSelection)
   813	            {
   814	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(_selectedValues.FirstOrDefault());
   815	            }
   816	            else
   817	            {
   818	                //Warning. Here the Converter was not set yet
   819	                if (MultiSelectionTextFunc != null)
   820	                {
   821	                    await SetCustomizedTextAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)),
   822	                        selectedConvertedValues: _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet).ToList(),
   823	                        multiSelectionTextFunc: MultiSelectionTextFunc);
   824	                }
   825	                else
   826	                {
   827	                    await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)), updateValue: false);
   828	                }
   829	            }
   830	
   831	            // Only fire FieldChanged after the first render to avoid triggering during initialization
   832	            if (HasRendered)
   833	            {
   834	                FieldChanged(_selectedValues);
   835	            }
   836	
   837	            if (MultiSelection && typeof(T) == typeof(string))
   838	            {
   839	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync((T?)(object?)ReadText, updateText: false);
   840	            }
   841	        }
   842	
   843	        internal void UpdateFitContent()
   844	        {
   845	            if (FitContent)
   846	            {
   847	                var longestItemLength = 0;
   848	                var longestItem = default(MudSelectItem<T>);
   849	                foreach (var item in _context.ShadowItems)
   850	                {
   851	                    var value = item.Value;
   852	                    var valueToString = ConvertSet(value);
   853	                    var length = valueToString?.Length ?? 0;
   854	
   855	                    if (length > longestItemLength)
   856	                    {
   857	                        longestItem = item;
   858	                        longestItemLength = length;
   859	                    }
   860	                }
   861	
   862	                if (ReferenceEquals(_longestItem, longestItem))
   863	                {
   864	                    return;
   865	                }
   866	
   867	                _longestItem = longestItem;
   868	                StateHasChanged();
   869	                return;
   870	            }
   871	
   872	            _longestItem = null;
   873	        }
   874	
   875	        internal void InvalidateFitContent()
   876	        {
   877	            if (FitContent)
   878	            {
   879	                _needsFitContentRefresh = true;
   880	            }
   881	        }
   882	
   883	        private void OnFitContentChanged(ParameterChangedEventArgs<bool> args)
   884	        {
   885	            if (args.Value)
   886	            {
   887	                UpdateFitContent();
   888	                return;
   889	            }
   890	
   891	            _needsFitContentRefresh = false;
   892	            _longestItem = null;
   893	        }
   894	
   895	        private void UpdateIcon()
   896	        {
   897	            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(AdornmentIcon))
   898	            {
   899	                _currentIcon = AdornmentIcon;
   900	                return;
   901	            }
   902	
   903	            _currentIcon = _openState.Value ? CloseIcon : OpenIcon;
   904	        }
   905	
   906	        private Task HighlightItemForValueAsync(T? value)
   907	        {
   908	            _context.TryGetItemByValue(value, out var item);
   909	            return HighlightItemAsync(item);
   910	        }
   911	
   912	        private Task HighlightItemAsync(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   913	        {
   914	            _activeItemId = item?.ItemId;
   915	            return InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   916	        }
   917	
   918	        private void UpdateSelectAllChecked()
   919	        {
   920	            if (MultiSelection && SelectAll)
   921	            {
   922	                if (_selectedValues.Count == 0)
   923	                {
   924	                    _selectAllChecked = false;
   925	                }
   926	                else if (Items.Count(x => !x.Disabled) == _selectedValues.Count)
   927	                {
   928	                    _selectAllChecked = true;
   929	                }
   930	                else
   931	                {
   932	                    _selectAllChecked = null;
   933	                }
   934	            }
   935	        }
   936	
   937	        private async Task SelectAllClickAsync()
   938	        {
   939	            // Manage the fake tri-state of a checkbox
   940	            if (!_selectAllChecked.HasValue)
   941	            {
   942	                _selectAllChecked = true;
   943	            }
   944	            else if (_selectAllChecked.Value)
   945	            {
   946	                _selectAllChecked = false;
   947	            }
   948	            else
   949	            {
   950	                _selectAllChecked = true;
   951	            }
   952	
   953	            // Define the items selection
   954	            if (_selectAllChecked.Value)
   955	            {
   956	                await SelectAllItems();
   957	            }
   958	            else
   959	            {
   960	                await ClearAsync();
   961	            }
   962	        }
   963	
   964	        private async Task SelectAllItems()
   965	        {
   966	            if (!MultiSelection)
   967	            {
   968	                return;
   969	            }
   970	
   971	            var selectedValues = new HashSet<T?>(Items.Where(x => !x.Disabled && x.Value != null).Select(x => x.Value), Comparer);
   972	            _selectedValues = new HashSet<T?>(selectedValues, Comparer);
   973	
   974	            if (MultiSelectionTextFunc != null)
   975	            {
   976	                await SetCustomizedTextAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)),
   977	                    selectedConvertedValues: _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet).ToList(),
   978	                    multiSelectionTextFunc: MultiSelectionTextFunc);
   979	            }
   980	            else
   981	            {
   982	                await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)), updateValue: false);
   983	            }
   984	
   985	            UpdateSelectAllChecked();
   986	            _selectedValues = selectedValues; // need to force selected values because Blazor overwrites it under certain circumstances due to changes of Text or Value
   987	            await BeginValidateAsync();
   988	            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync();
   989	            FieldChanged(_selectedValues);
   990	
   991	            if (MultiSelection && typeof(T) == typeof(string))
   992	            {
   993	                SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync((T?)(object?)ReadText, updateText: false).CatchAndLog();
   994	            }
   995	        }
   996	
   997	        private async Task OnFocusOutAsync()
   998	        {
   999	            if (_openState.Value)
  1000	            {
  1001	                // when the menu is open we immediately get back the focus if we lose it (i.e. because of checkboxes in multi-select)
  1002	                // otherwise we can't receive key strokes any longer
  1003	                await FocusAsync();
  1004	            }
  1005	        }
  1006	
  1007	        private Task SelectNextItem() => SelectAdjacentItem(+1);
  1008	
  1009	        private Task SelectPreviousItem() => SelectAdjacentItem(-1);
  1010	
  1011	        private async Task SelectAdjacentItem(int direction)
  1012	        {
  1013	            if (Items.Count == 0)
  1014	            {
  1015	                return;
  1016	            }
  1017	
  1018	            var index = Items.FindIndex(x => x.ItemId == _activeItemId);
  1019	            if (direction < 0 && index < 0)
  1020	            {
  1021	                index = 0;
  1022	            }
  1023	
  1024	            MudSelectItem<T>? item = null;
  1025	            // the loop allows us to jump over disabled items until we reach the next non-disabled one
  1026	            for (var i = 0; i < Items.Count; i++)
  1027	            {
  1028	                index += direction;
  1029	                if (index < 0)
  1030	                {
  1031	                    index = 0;
  1032	                }
  1033	
  1034	                if (index >= Items.Count)
  1035	                {
  1036	                    index = Items.Count - 1;
  1037	                }
  1038	
  1039	                if (Items[index].Disabled)
  1040	                {
  1041	                    continue;
  1042	                }
  1043	
  1044	                item = Items[index];
  1045	                if (!MultiSelection)
  1046	                {
  1047	                    // When SelectionOnEnter is true, we only update the visual highlight during navigation.
  1048	                    // When false (default), the value is immediately updated as the user moves through the list.
  1049	                    if (!SelectionOnEnter)
  1050	                    {
  1051	                        _selectedValues.Clear();
  1052	                        _selectedValues.Add(item.Value);
  1053	                        await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(item.Value, updateText: true);
  1054	                    }
  1055	
  1056	                    await HighlightItemAsync(item);
  1057	                    break;
  1058	                }
  1059	
  1060	                // in multiselect mode don't select anything, just highlight.
  1061	                // selecting is done by Enter
  1062	                await HighlightItemAsync(item);
  1063	                break;
  1064	            }
  1065	
  1066	            await _elementReference.SetText(ReadText);
  1067	            await ScrollToItemAsync(item);
  1068	        }
  1069	
  1070	        private ValueTask ScrollToItemAsync(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
  1071	            => item != null ? ScrollManager.ScrollToListItemAsync(item.ItemId) : ValueTask.CompletedTask;
  1072	
  1073	        private async Task SelectFirstItem(string? startChar = null)
  1074	        {
  1075	            IReadOnlyCollection<MudSelectItem<T>> selectList = Items;
  1076	
  1077	            if (!_openState.Value)
  1078	            {
  1079	                // When closed, use shadow lookup to include all items (visible + hidden)
  1080	                selectList = _context.ShadowItems;
  1081	            }
  1082	
  1083	            if (selectList.Count == 0)
  1084	            {
  1085	                return;
  1086	            }
  1087	
  1088	            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(startChar))
  1089	            {
  1090	                // SelectItemBySearch handles disabled items
  1091	                var searchItem = SelectItemBySearch(selectList, startChar);
  1092	                if (searchItem is not null)
  1093	                {
  1094	                    await SelectAndHighlightItemAsync(searchItem);
  1095	                    return;
  1096	                }
  1097	            }
  1098	
  1099	            // Find first non-disabled item
  1100	            foreach (var item in selectList)
  1101	            {
  1102	                if (item.Disabled)
  1103	                {
  1104	                    continue;
  1105	                }
  1106	
  1107	                await SelectAndHighlightItemAsync(item);
  1108	                return;
  1109	            }
  1110	        }
  1111	
  1112	        private MudSelectItem<T>? SelectItemBySearch(IReadOnlyCollection<MudSelectItem<T>> items, string inputChar)
  1113	        {
  1114	            UpdateSearchText(inputChar);
  1115	
  1116	            MudSelectItem<T>? activeItem = null;
  1117	            MudSelectItem<T>? previousItem = null;
  1118	            MudSelectItem<T>? firstMatch = null;
  1119	            MudSelectItem<T>? nextMatch = null;
  1120	            var foundPrevious = false;
  1121	
  1122	            foreach (var item in items)
  1123	            {
  1124	                TrackSpecialItems(item, ref activeItem, ref previousItem);
  1125	
  1126	                if (IsMatch(item))
  1127	                {
  1128	                    firstMatch ??= item;
  1129	
  1130	                    if (foundPrevious)
  1131	                    {
  1132	                        nextMatch ??= item;
  1133	                    }
  1134	
  1135	                    if (item == previousItem)
  1136	                    {
  1137	                        foundPrevious = true;
  1138	                    }
  1139	                }
  1140	            }
  1141	
  1142	            return DetermineResult(activeItem, previousItem, firstMatch, nextMatch);
  1143	
  1144	            void UpdateSearchText(string input)
  1145	            {
  1146	                var now = TimeProvider.GetUtcNow();
  1147	
  1148	                if (now - _lastSearchTime > QuickSearchInterval)
  1149	                {
  1150	                    _lastSelectedId = _activeItemId;
  1151	                    _searchText = input;
  1152	                }
  1153	                else
  1154	                {
  1155	                    _searchText += input;
  1156	                }
  1157	
  1158	                _lastSearchTime = now;
  1159	            }
  1160	
  1161	            void TrackSpecialItems(MudSelectItem<T> item, ref MudSelectItem<T>? active, ref MudSelectItem<T>? previous)
  1162	            {
  1163	                if (item.ItemId == _activeItemId)
  1164	                {
  1165	                    active = item;
  1166	                }
  1167	
  1168	                if (item.ItemId == _lastSelectedId)
  1169	                {
  1170	                    previous = item;
  1171	                }
  1172	            }
  1173	
  1174	            bool IsMatch(MudSelectItem<T> item)
  1175	            {
  1176	                if (item.Disabled)
  1177	                {
  1178	                    return false;
  1179	                }
  1180	
  1181	                var text = ConvertSet(item.Value);
  1182	                return text is not null && text.StartsWith(_searchText, StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase);
  1183	            }
  1184	
  1185	            MudSelectItem<T>? DetermineResult(MudSelectItem<T>? active, MudSelectItem<T>? previous,
  1186	                                               MudSelectItem<T>? first, MudSelectItem<T>? next)
  1187	            {
  1188	                if (first is null)
  1189	                {
  1190	                    return active;
  1191	                }
  1192	
  1193	                if (previous is null)
  1194	                {
  1195	                    return first;
  1196	                }
  1197	
  1198	                return next ?? first;
  1199	            }
  1200	        }
  1201	
  1202	        private async Task SelectAndHighlightItemAsync(MudSelectItem<T> item)
  1203	        {
  1204	            if (!MultiSelection)
  1205	            {
  1206	                _selectedValues.Clear();
  1207	                _selectedValues.Add(item.Value);
  1208	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(item.Value, updateText: true);
  1209	                await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync();
  1210	            }
  1211	
  1212	            await HighlightItemAsync(item);
  1213	            await _elementReference.SetText(ReadText);
  1214	            await ScrollToItemAsync(item);
  1215	        }
  1216	
  1217	        private async Task SelectLastItem()
  1218	        {
  1219	            if (Items.Count == 0)
  1220	            {
  1221	                return;
  1222	            }
  1223	
  1224	            var item = Items.LastOrDefault(x => !x.Disabled);
  1225	            if (item == null)
  1226	            {
  1227	                return;
  1228	            }
  1229	
  1230	            if (!MultiSelection)
  1231	            {
  1232	                _selectedValues.Clear();
  1233	                _selectedValues.Add(item.Value);
  1234	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(item.Value, updateText: true);
  1235	            }
  1236	
  1237	            await HighlightItemAsync(item);
  1238	            await _elementReference.SetText(ReadText);
  1239	            await ScrollToItemAsync(item);
  1240	        }

  1341	        private async Task HandleCharacterSearchAsync(KeyboardEventArgs args)
  1342	        {

  1381	        protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
  1382	        {

  1384	            {
  1385	                var options = new KeyInterceptorOptions(
  1386	                    "mud-input-control",
  1387	                    [
  1388	                        // prevent scrolling page, toggle open/close
  1389	                        new(" ", preventDown: "key+none"),
  1390	                        // prevent scrolling page, instead highlight previous item
  1391	                        new("ArrowUp", preventDown: "key+none"),

  1397	                        new("Enter", preventDown: "key+none"),
  1398	                        new("NumpadEnter", preventDown: "key+none"),
  1399	                        // select all items instead of all page text
  1400	                        new("a", preventDown: "key+ctrl"),
  1401	                        // select all items instead of all page text
  1402	                        new("A", preventDown: "key+ctrl"),
  1403	                        // for our users
  1404	                        new("/./", subscribeDown: true, subscribeUp: true)
  1405	                    ]);
  1406	
  1407	                await KeyInterceptorService.SubscribeAsync(ElementId, options, keys => keys
  1408	                    .HookKeyUp(args => OnKeyUp.InvokeAsync(args))
  1409	                    .When(CanHandleKeys, builder => builder
  1410	                        .HookKeyDown(args => OnKeyDown.InvokeAsync(args))
  1411	                        .OnKeyDown("Tab", () => CloseMenu(false))
  1412	                        .OnKeyDown("ArrowUp", HandleArrowUpAsync)
  1413	                        .OnKeyDown("ArrowDown", HandleArrowDownAsync)
  1414	                        .OnKeyDown(" ", ToggleMenu)
  1415	                        .OnKeyDown("Escape", () => CloseMenu(true))
  1416	                        .OnKeyDown("Home", () => SelectFirstItem())
  1417	                        .OnKeyDown("End", SelectLastItem)
  1418	                        .OnKeyDownAny(["Enter", "NumpadEnter"], HandleEnterAsync)
  1419	                        .OnKeyDownAny(["a", "A"], HandleKeyAAsync)
  1420	                        .OnKeyDown("/^[^ ]$/", HandleCharacterSearchAsync)));
  1421	            }
  1422	
  1423	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
  1424	
  1425	            var needsFitContentRefresh = _needsFitContentRefresh;
  1426	            _needsFitContentRefresh = false;
  1427	
  1428	            if (needsFitContentRefresh)
  1429	            {
  1430	                UpdateFitContent();
  1431	            }
  1432	            else if (firstRender)
  1433	            {
  1434	                // we need to render the initial Value which is not possible without the items
  1435	                // which supply the RenderFragment. So in this case, a second render is necessary
  1436	                StateHasChanged();
  1437	            }
  1438	
  1439	            UpdateSelectAllChecked();
  1440	
  1441	            // Highlight after items are fully rendered
  1442	            if (_needsHighlightAfterRender)
  1443	            {
  1444	                _needsHighlightAfterRender = false;
  1445	                await InvokeAsync(async () =>
  1446	                {
  1447	                    if (MultiSelection)
  1448	                    {
  1449	                        var firstNonDisabled = Items.FirstOrDefault(x => !x.Disabled);
  1450	                        await HighlightItemAsync(firstNonDisabled);
  1451	                    }
  1452	                    else
  1453	                    {
  1454	                        await HighlightItemForValueAsync(ReadValue);
  1455	                    }
  1456	                });
  1457	            }
  1458	        }
  1459	
  1460	        /// <summary>
  1461	        /// Gets the resolved modal overlay value, using the global default from <see cref="PopoverOptions"/> if not explicitly set.
  1462	        /// </summary>
  1463	        protected bool GetModal() => Modal ?? PopoverService.PopoverOptions.ModalOverlay;
  1464	
  1465	        protected RenderFragment? GetSelectedValuePresenter()
  1466	        {
  1467	            if (!_context.TryGetShadowItemByValue(ReadValue, out var item))
  1468	            {
  1469	                return null; //<-- for now. we'll add a custom template to present values (set from outside) which are not on the list?
  1470	            }
  1471	
  1472	            return item.ChildContent;
  1473	        }
  1474	
  1475	        /// <summary>
  1476	        /// Occurs when the <c>Clear</c> button has been clicked.
  1477	        /// </summary>
  1478	        /// <remarks>
  1479	        /// This is the first event raised when the clear button is clicked.
  1480	        /// The <see cref="SelectedValues"/> are cleared and the <see cref="OnClearButtonClick"/> event is raised.
  1481	        /// </remarks>
  1482	        protected async ValueTask SelectClearButtonClickHandlerAsync(MouseEventArgs e)
  1483	        {
  1484	            await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(default, false);
  1485	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(null, false);
  1486	            _selectedValues.Clear();
  1487	            await BeginValidateAsync();
  1488	            StateHasChanged();
  1489	            await UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync();
  1490	            FieldChanged(_selectedValues);
  1491	            await OnClearButtonClick.InvokeAsync(e);
  1492	        }
  1493	
  1494	        private async Task UpdateSelectedValuesStateAsync(IEqualityComparer<T?>? comparer = null)
  1495	        {
  1496	            await _selectedValuesState.SetValueAsync(new HashSet<T?>(_selectedValues, comparer ?? Comparer));
  1497	            await _context.NotifySelectionChangedAsync();
  1498	        }
  1499	
  1500	        protected async Task SetCustomizedTextAsync(string text, bool updateValue = true,
  1501	            IReadOnlyList<string?>? selectedConvertedValues = null,
  1502	            Func<IReadOnlyList<string?>?, string>? multiSelectionTextFunc = null)
  1503	        {
  1504	            // The Text property of the control is updated
  1505	            var customText = multiSelectionTextFunc?.Invoke(selectedConvertedValues);
  1506	            await SetTextCoreAsync(customText);
  1507	
  1508	            // The comparison is made on the multiSelectionText variable
  1509	            if (_multiSelectionText != text)
  1510	            {
  1511	                _multiSelectionText = text;
  1512	                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_multiSelectionText))
  1513	                {
  1514	                    Touched = true;
  1515	                }
  1516	
  1517	                if (updateValue)
  1518	                {
  1519	                    await UpdateValuePropertyAsync(false);
  1520	                }
  1521	            }
  1522	        }
  1523	
  1524	        /// <remarks>
  1525	        /// If <see cref="ToStringFunc"/> is set, it is used to convert the value to a string; otherwise, the base implementation is used.
  1526	        /// </remarks>
  1527	        /// <inheritdoc />
  1528	        protected override string? ConvertSet(T? input)
  1529	        {
  1530	            return ToStringFunc is not null
  1531	                ? ToStringFunc(input)
  1532	                : base.ConvertSet(input);
  1533	        }
  1534	
  1535	        protected override Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
  1536	        {
  1537	            // For MultiSelection of non-string T's we don't update the Value!!!
  1538	            if (typeof(T) == typeof(string) || !MultiSelection)
  1539	            {
  1540	                base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
  1541	            }
  1542	
  1543	            return Task.CompletedTask;
  1544	        }
  1545	
  1546	        protected override Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
  1547	        {
  1548	            // when multiselection is true, we return
  1549	            // a comma separated list of selected values
  1550	            if (MultiSelectionTextFunc != null)
  1551	            {
  1552	                return MultiSelection
  1553	                    ? SetCustomizedTextAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)),
  1554	                        selectedConvertedValues: _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet).ToList(),
  1555	                        multiSelectionTextFunc: MultiSelectionTextFunc)
  1556	                    : base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
  1557	            }
  1558	
  1559	            return MultiSelection
  1560	                ? SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Join(Delimiter, _selectedValues.Select(ConvertSet)))
  1561	                : base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
  1562	        }
  1563	
  1564	        /// <summary>
  1565	        /// Clears all selections and resets validation
  1566	        /// </summary>
  1567	        /// <remarks>
  1568	        /// To maintain validation errors (e.g. required), use <see cref="ClearAsync"/>
  1569	        /// </remarks>
  1570	        protected override async Task ResetValueAsync()
  1571	        {
  1572	            await ClearAsync();
  1573	            await base.ResetValueAsync();
  1574	        }
  1575	
  1576	        /// <summary>
  1577	        /// Gets whether the value is currently selected.
  1578	        /// </summary>
  1579	        /// <param name="value">The value to test.</param>
  1580	        /// <returns>When <c>true</c>, the specified value exists in <see cref="SelectedValues"/>.</returns>
  1581	        protected override bool HasValue(T? value)
  1582	        {
  1583	            // Fixes issue #4328
  1584	            if (MultiSelection)
  1585	            {
  1586	                return _selectedValues.Count != 0;
  1587	            }
  1588	
  1589	            return base.HasValue(value);
  1590	        }
  1591	
  1592	        /// <inheritdoc />
  1593	        protected override async ValueTask DisposeAsyncCore()
  1594	        {
  1595	            await base.DisposeAsyncCore();
  1596	
  1597	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable)
  1598	            {
  1599	                await KeyInterceptorService.UnsubscribeAsync(ElementId);
  1600	            }
  1601	        }
  1602	    }
  1603	}
--- razor ---

     5	<CascadingValue Name="SubscribeToParentForm" Value="false" IsFixed="true">
     6	    <div class="@OuterClassname" id="@ElementId" @onfocusout="@OnFocusOutAsync" @onclick:stopPropagation @onmousedown:stopPropagation>
     7	        <MudInputControl Label="@Label"
     8	                         Variant="@Variant"
     9	                         HelperId="@GetHelperId()"
    10	                         HelperText="@HelperText"
    11	                         HelperTextOnFocus="@HelperTextOnFocus"
    12	                         FullWidth="@FullWidth"
    13	                         Margin="@Margin"
    14	                         Class="@Classname"
    15	                         Style="@Style"
    16	                         Error="@HasErrors"
    17	                         ErrorId="@ErrorIdState.Value"
    18	                         ErrorText="@GetErrorText()"
    19	                         Disabled="@GetDisabledState()"
    20	                         Required="@Required"
    21	                         ForId="@InputElementId"
    22	                         @onmousedown="@HandleMouseDown">
    23	            <InputContent>
    24	                <MudInput @ref="_elementReference"
    25	                          InputType="@(CanRenderValue || (Strict && !IsValueInList) ? InputType.Hidden : InputType.Text)"
    26	                          Class="@InputClassname"
    27	                          Margin="@Margin"
    28	                          Placeholder="@Placeholder"
    29	                          Label="@Label"
    30	                          Variant="@Variant"
    31	                          Typo="@Typo"
    32	                          Value="@(Strict && !IsValueInList ? null : ReadText)"
    33	                          Underline="@Underline"
    34	                          Disabled="@GetDisabledState()"
    35	                          ReadOnly="true"
    36	                          Error="@HasErrors"
    37	                          ErrorId="@ErrorIdState.Value"
    38	                          HelperId="@GetHelperId()"
    39	                          HelperText="@HelperText"
    40	                          AdornmentText="@AdornmentText"
    41	                          AdornmentIcon="@_currentIcon"
    42	                          Adornment="@Adornment"
    43	                          AdornmentColor="@AdornmentColor"
    44	                          IconSize="@IconSize"
    45	                          AdornmentAriaLabel="@AdornmentAriaLabel"
    46	                          OnAdornmentClick="@OnAdornmentClick"
    47	                          Clearable="@(Clearable && !GetReadOnlyState())"
    48	                          ClearIcon="@ClearIcon"
    49	                          OnClearButtonClick="@(async (e) => await SelectClearButtonClickHandlerAsync(e))"
    50	                          @attributes="GetInputUserAttributes()"
    51	                          OnBlur="@OnBlurAsync"
    52	                          ShrinkLabel="@(ShrinkLabel || CanRenderValue)"
    53	                          InputId="@InputElementId"
    54	                          Required="@Required">
    55	                    @if (CanRenderValue)
    56	                    {
    57	                        @GetSelectedValuePresenter()
    58	                    }
    59	                </MudInput>
    60	                @if (FitContent)
    61	                {
    62	                    <MudStack Class="@FillerClassname" Spacing="1" Row>
    63	                        @{
    64	                            var value = string.Empty;
    65	
    66	                            if (_longestItem is { Value: not null })
    67	                            {
    68	                                value = ConvertSet(_longestItem.Value) ?? string.Empty;
    69	                            }
    70	
    71	                            var useLabel = Label is not null && Placeholder is null && !ShrinkLabel 
    72	                                        && (Adornment != Adornment.Start || (AdornmentIcon is null && AdornmentText is null));
    73	
    74	                            var defaultValue = useLabel ? Label : Placeholder;
    75	                            var showDefault = defaultValue?.Length > value.Length;
    76	                            var hasChildContent = _longestItem?.ChildContent is not null;
    77	                            var hasStringValue = ToStringFunc is not null && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(value);
    78	
    79	                            var renderText = showDefault || !hasChildContent || MultiSelectionTextFunc is not null || hasStringValue;
    80	                        }
    81	
    82	                        @if (renderText)
    83	                        {
    84	                            var text = showDefault ? defaultValue! : value;
    85	
    86	                            <MudText Typo="@Typo">
    87	                                @(MultiSelectionTextFunc?.Invoke([text]) ?? text)
    88	                            </MudText>
    89	                        }
    90	                        else
    91	                        {
    92	                            <MudText Typo="@Typo">@_longestItem!.ChildContent</MudText>
    93	                        }
    94	
    95	                        @AdornmentText
    96	
    97	                        @if (AdornmentText is null)
    98	                        {
    99	                            <MudIcon Icon="@(AdornmentIcon ?? OpenIcon)" Size="IconSize"></MudIcon>
   100	                        }
   101	
   102	                        @if (Clearable)
   103	                        {
   104	                            <MudIcon Icon="@ClearIcon" Size="IconSize"></MudIcon>
   105	                        }
   106	                    </MudStack>
   107	                }
   108	                <MudPopover Open="@_openState.Value"
   109	                            MaxHeight="@MaxHeight"
   110	                            Class="@PopoverClass"
   111	                            AnchorOrigin="@AnchorOrigin"
   112	                            TransformOrigin="@TransformOrigin"
   113	                            Fixed="@PopoverFixed"
   114	                            RelativeWidth="@RelativeWidth">
   115	                    <CascadingValue Value="@((IMudSelect)this)" IsFixed="true">
   116	                        <MudList T="string"
   117	                                 @attributes="GetListUserAttributes()"
   118	                                 Class="@ListClass"
   119	                                 Dense="@Dense"
   120	                                 @bind-SelectedValue="_activeItemId">
   121	                            @if (MultiSelection && SelectAll)
   122	                            {
   123	                                <MudListItem Value="@("__SelectAll__")"
   124	                                             Icon="@SelectAllCheckBoxIcon"
   125	                                             Text="@SelectAllText"
   126	                                             OnClick="SelectAllClickAsync"
   127	                                             OnClickPreventDefault="true"
   128	                                             Dense="@Dense"
   129	                                             Class="mb-2" />
   130	                                <MudDivider />
   131	                            }
   132	                            @ChildContent
   133	                        </MudList>
   134	                    </CascadingValue>
   135	                </MudPopover>
   136	            </InputContent>
   137	        </MudInputControl>
   138	    </div>
   139	    @*Shadow select items for IsValueInList and CanRenderValue*@
   140	    <CascadingValue Value="@((IMudShadowSelect)this)" IsFixed="true">
   141	        <CascadingValue Name="HideContent" Value="true">
   142	            @ChildContent
   143	        </CascadingValue>
   144	    </CascadingValue>
   145	</CascadingValue>
   146	<!-- 
   147	pointerdown instead of click needed to close the menu before OnLostFocus runs
   148	
   149	When Modal is false the overlay does not receive pointer events so we activate
   150	the auto close feature and call CloseMenu in OnClosed. The modeless auto close
   151	feature relies on pointerdown event resulting in the same order of events.
   152	-->
   153	<MudOverlay Visible="_openState.Value"
   154	            @onpointerdown="@(() => CloseMenu(false))"
   155	            data-modeless-ignore-element-id="@ElementId"
   156	            LockScroll="@LockScroll"
   157	            AutoClose="@(!GetModal())"
   158	            Modal="@GetModal()"
   159	            OnClosed="@(() => CloseMenu(false))"/>

     1	﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     2	using MudBlazor.State;
     3	using MudBlazor.Utilities;
     4	
     5	namespace MudBlazor
     6	{
     7	    /// <summary>
     8	    /// A selectable option displayed within a <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> component.
     9	    /// </summary>
    10	    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of value linked to this item.  Must be the same type as the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>.</typeparam>
    11	    /// <seealso cref="MudSelect{T}"/>
    12	    public partial class MudSelectItem<T> : MudComponentBase, IDisposable
    13	    {
    14	        private MudSelectContext<T>? _context;
    15	        private MudSelectContext<T>? _shadowContext;
    16	        private IDisposable? _selectionSubscription;
    17	
    18	        private string GetCssClasses() => new CssBuilder()
    19	            .AddClass(Class)
    20	            .Build();
    21	
    22	        internal string ItemId { get; } = Identifier.Create();
    23	
    24	        /// <summary>
    25	        /// Builds fallback accessibility attributes for the rendered option element.
    26	        /// </summary>
    27	        /// <remarks>
    28	        /// Option semantics come from this item's selection state rather than the popup's temporary active item.
    29	        /// </remarks>
    30	        private Dictionary<string, object?> GetUserAttributes()
    31	        {
    32	            var attributes = new Dictionary<string, object?>(UserAttributes, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    33	            attributes.TryAdd("aria-selected", Selected ? "true" : "false");
    34	
    35	            if (Disabled)
    36	            {
    37	                attributes.TryAdd("aria-disabled", "true");
    38	            }
    39	
    40	            return attributes;
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        public MudSelectItem()
    44	        {
    45	            using var registerScope = CreateRegisterScope();
    46	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<IMudSelect?>(nameof(IMudSelect))
    47	                .WithParameter(() => IMudSelect)
    48	                .WithChangeHandler(OnMudSelectChanged);
    49	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<IMudShadowSelect?>(nameof(IMudShadowSelect))
    50	                .WithParameter(() => IMudShadowSelect)
    51	                .WithChangeHandler(OnMudShadowSelectChanged);
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        /// <summary>
    55	        /// The <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> hosting this item.
    56	        /// </summary>
    57	        /// <remarks>
    58	        /// This cascading parameter is used to obtain the context for registration.
    59	        /// When this parameter changes, OnMudSelectChanged is invoked to handle
    60	        /// registration and unregistration with the appropriate parent.
    61	        /// </remarks>
    62	        [CascadingParameter]
    63	        internal IMudSelect? IMudSelect { get; set; }
    64	
    65	        /// <summary>
    66	        /// The shadow select used for items that only provide RenderFragments.
    67	        /// </summary>
    68	        /// <remarks>
    69	        /// Shadow items (HideContent=true) are registered in a separate lookup
    70	        /// for value-to-RenderFragment resolution when the dropdown is closed.
    71	        /// </remarks>
    72	        [CascadingParameter]
    73	        internal IMudShadowSelect? IMudShadowSelect { get; set; }
    74	
    75	        /// <summary>
    76	        /// Select items with HideContent==true are only there to register their RenderFragment with the select but
    77	        /// won't render and have no other purpose!
    78	        /// </summary>
    79	        [CascadingParameter(Name = "HideContent")]
    80	        internal bool HideContent { get; set; }
    81	
    82	        /// <summary>
    83	        /// Gets the parent MudSelect component.
    84	        /// </summary>
    85	        internal MudSelect<T>? MudSelect => (MudSelect<T>?)IMudSelect;
    86	
    87	        /// <summary>
    88	        /// The custom value associated with this item.
    89	        /// </summary>
    90	        [Parameter]
    91	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
    92	        public T? Value { get; set; }
    93	
    94	        /// <summary>
    95	        /// Prevents the user from interacting with this item.
    96	        /// </summary>
    97	        /// <remarks>
    98	        /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.
    99	        /// </remarks>
   100	        [Parameter]
   101	        [Category(CategoryTypes.General.Behavior)]
   102	        public bool Disabled { get; set; }
   103	
   104	        /// <summary>
   105	        /// The custom content within this item.
   106	        /// </summary>
   107	        [Parameter]
   108	        [Category(CategoryTypes.General.Behavior)]
   109	        public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
   110	
   111	        /// <summary>
   112	        /// Whether multi-selection is enabled in the parent <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/>.
   113	        /// </summary>
   114	        protected bool MultiSelection => _context?.MultiSelection == true;
   115	
   116	        /// <summary>
   117	        /// Whether this item is selected.
   118	        /// </summary>
   119	        /// <remarks>
   120	        /// <para>
   121	        /// This state is updated by observing the parent's selection via the context.
   122	        /// Items subscribe to selection changes and update this state accordingly.
   123	        /// </para>
   124	        /// </remarks>
   125	        internal bool Selected { get; set; }
   126	
   127	        /// <summary>
   128	        /// The icon to display whether this item is selected.
   129	        /// </summary>
   130	        /// <remarks>
   131	        /// When <see cref="Selected"/> is <c>true</c>, <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.CheckBox"/> is returned.  Otherwise, <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.CheckBoxOutlineBlank"/>.
   132	        /// </remarks>
   133	        protected string? CheckBoxIcon
   134	        {
   135	            get
   136	            {
   137	                if (!MultiSelection)
   138	                    return null;
   139	                return Selected ? Icons.Material.Filled.CheckBox : Icons.Material.Filled.CheckBoxOutlineBlank;
   140	            }
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        protected string DisplayString
   144	        {
   145	            get
   146	            {
   147	                // Use the parent's ConvertValueToString which delegates to ConvertSet (handles ToStringFunc)
   148	                return MudSelect?.ConvertValueToString(Value) ?? $"{Value}";
   149	            }
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        /// <summary>
   153	        /// Handles changes to the IMudShadowSelect cascading parameter.
   154	        /// </summary>
   155	        /// <remarks>
   156	        /// This is invoked when the shadow select parent changes (e.g., when moving between different selects).
   157	        /// It unregisters from the old parent and registers with the new one.
   158	        /// </remarks>
   159	        private void OnMudShadowSelectChanged(ParameterChangedEventArgs<IMudShadowSelect?> args)
   160	        {
   161	            if (args.LastValue?.SelectContext is MudSelectContext<T> oldContext)
   162	            {
   163	                oldContext.UnregisterShadowItem(this);
   164	            }
   165	
   166	            if (args.Value?.SelectContext is MudSelectContext<T> newContext)
   167	            {
   168	                _shadowContext = newContext;
   169	                _shadowContext.RegisterShadowItem(this);
   170	            }
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        /// <summary>
   174	        /// Handles changes to the IMudSelect cascading parameter.
   175	        /// </summary>
   176	        /// <remarks>
   177	        /// <para>
   178	        /// This is invoked when the select parent changes (e.g., when moving between different selects).
   179	        /// It handles the complete lifecycle:
   180	        /// </para>
   181	        /// <list type="number">
   182	        /// <item><description>Unsubscribes from the old parent's selection changes</description></item>
   183	        /// <item><description>Unregisters from the old parent's context</description></item>
   184	        /// <item><description>Registers with the new parent's context</description></item>
   185	        /// <item><description>Subscribes to the new parent's selection changes</description></item>
   186	        /// <item><description>Updates the initial Selected state</description></item>
   187	        /// </list>
   188	        /// </remarks>
   189	        private void OnMudSelectChanged(ParameterChangedEventArgs<IMudSelect?> args)
   190	        {
   191	            if (args.LastValue?.SelectContext is MudSelectContext<T> oldContext)
   192	            {
   193	                _selectionSubscription?.Dispose();
   194	                _selectionSubscription = null;
   195	                oldContext.UnregisterItem(this);
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            if (args.Value?.SelectContext is MudSelectContext<T> newContext)
   199	            {
   200	                _context = newContext;
   201	
   202	                // Register as a visible item (adds to _items, _valueLookup, and _shadowLookup)
   203	                var isSelected = _context.RegisterItem(this);
   204	                Selected = isSelected;
   205	
   206	                _selectionSubscription = _context.SubscribeToSelectionChanges(OnSelectionChangedAsync);
   207	            }
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        /// <summary>
   211	        /// Handles selection changes from the parent select.
   212	        /// </summary>
   213	        /// <remarks>
   214	        /// This callback is invoked when the parent's SelectedValues changes.
   215	        /// It updates the local Selected state and triggers a re-render if needed.
   216	        /// This replaces the OnUpdateSelectionStateFromOutside method.
   217	        /// </remarks>
   218	        private Task OnSelectionChangedAsync(IReadOnlyCollection<T?> selectedValues)
   219	        {
   220	            var oldSelected = Selected;
   221	            Selected = selectedValues.Contains(Value);
   222	
   223	            if (oldSelected != Selected)
   224	            {
   225	                // Avoid await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged) due to a MAUI dispatcher bug:
   226	                // https://github.com/MudBlazor/MudBlazor/issues/13009
   227	                // This issue does not occur on other platforms (e.g., WASM, WinForms Hybrid, etc).
   228	                StateHasChanged();
   229	            }
   230	
   231	            return Task.CompletedTask;
   232	        }
   233	
   234	        /// <summary>
   235	        /// Handles click events on the item.
   236	        /// </summary>
   237	        private async Task OnClickHandleAsync()
   238	        {
   239	            if (MudSelect is not null)
   240	            {
   241	                await MudSelect.SelectOption(Value);
   242	            }
   243	        }
   244	
   245	        /// <inheritdoc />
   246	        public void Dispose()
   247	        {
   248	            Dispose(true);
   249	            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   250	        }
   251	
   252	        /// <summary>
   253	        /// Releases resources used by this component.
   254	        /// </summary>
   255	        protected virtual void Dispose(bool disposing)
   256	        {
   257	            if (!disposing)
   258	            {
   259	                return;
   260	            }
--- context ---
     1	﻿// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021
     2	// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
     3	// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.
     4	
     5	using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;
     6	using MudBlazor.Extensions;
     7	using MudBlazor.Utilities;
     8	
     9	namespace MudBlazor;
    10	
    11	/// <summary>
    12	/// Manages the communication between <see cref="MudSelect{T}"/> and <see cref="MudSelectItem{T}"/> components.
    13	/// </summary>
    14	/// <typeparam name="T">The type of value being selected.</typeparam>
    15	internal sealed class MudSelectContext<T>
    16	{
    17	    private readonly MudSelect<T> _select;
    18	    private readonly List<MudSelectItem<T>> _items = [];
    19	    private readonly List<Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>> _selectionObservers = [];
    20	    private readonly Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _valueLookup = new();
    21	    private readonly Dictionary<NullableObject<T?>, MudSelectItem<T>> _shadowLookup = new();
    22	
    23	    /// <summary>
    24	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="MudSelectContext{T}"/> class.
    25	    /// </summary>
    26	    /// <param name="select">The parent select component.</param>
    27	    public MudSelectContext(MudSelect<T> select)
    28	    {
    29	        _select = select;
    30	    }
    31	
    32	    /// <summary>
    33	    /// Gets the ordered list of all visible items in the dropdown.
    34	    /// </summary>
    35	    /// <remarks>
    36	    /// Exposed as List to support FindIndex operations in the parent component.
    37	    /// </remarks>
    38	    public IReadOnlyList<MudSelectItem<T>> Items => _items;
    39	
    40	    /// <summary>
    41	    /// Gets all shadow items (including both visible and hidden items).
    42	    /// </summary>
    43	    public IReadOnlyCollection<MudSelectItem<T>> ShadowItems => _shadowLookup.Values;
    44	
    45	    /// <summary>
    46	    /// Gets whether multi-selection is enabled.
    47	    /// </summary>
    48	    public bool MultiSelection => _select.MultiSelection;
    49	
    50	    /// <summary>
    51	    /// Gets the current selected values.
    52	    /// </summary>
    53	    public IReadOnlyCollection<T?> SelectedValues => _select.GetSelectedValues() ?? Array.Empty<T?>();
    54	
    55	    /// <summary>
    56	    /// Registers an item as visible in the dropdown list.
    57	    /// </summary>
    58	    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
    59	    /// <returns><c>true</c> if the item is currently selected; otherwise <c>false</c>.</returns>
    60	    public bool RegisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
    61	    {
    62	        // Add to the ordered list of visible items
    63	        if (!_items.Contains(item))
    64	        {
    65	            _items.Add(item);
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        // Add to value lookup for fast access by value
    69	        _valueLookup[item.Value] = item;
    70	
    71	        // Note: Do NOT add to _shadowLookup here - that's only for shadow items
    72	        // Shadow items are registered separately via RegisterShadowItem
    73	
    74	        // Check if this item's value is currently selected
    75	        return _select.MultiSelection switch
    76	        {
    77	            true => _select.GetSelectedValues()?.Contains(item.Value) == true,
    78	            false => _select.ReadValue?.Equals(item.Value) == true
    79	        };
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    /// <summary>
    83	    /// Unregisters an item from the dropdown list.
    84	    /// </summary>
    85	    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
    86	    public void UnregisterItem(MudSelectItem<T> item)
    87	    {
    88	        _items.Remove(item);
    89	        _valueLookup.Remove(item.Value);
    90	        // Note: Do NOT remove from _shadowLookup - that's managed by shadow items
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    /// <summary>
    94	    /// Registers an item for value-to-RenderFragment lookup only (not visible in dropdown).
    95	    /// </summary>
    96	    /// <remarks>
    97	    /// Used for items with HideContent=true that provide RenderFragments for selected values
    98	    /// that may not be in the visible dropdown list.
    99	    /// </remarks>
   100	    /// <param name="item">The item to register.</param>
   101	    public void RegisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   102	    {
   103	        if (item is null)
   104	        {
   105	            return;
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        _shadowLookup[item.Value] = item;
   109	        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    /// <summary>
   113	    /// Unregisters a shadow item.
   114	    /// </summary>
   115	    /// <param name="item">The item to unregister.</param>
   116	    public void UnregisterShadowItem(MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   117	    {
   118	        if (item is null)
   119	        {
   120	            return;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        _shadowLookup.Remove(item.Value);
   124	        _select.InvalidateFitContent();
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    /// <summary>
   128	    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from visible items.
   129	    /// </summary>
   130	    public bool TryGetItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   131	    {
   132	        return _valueLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    /// <summary>
   136	    /// Attempts to get an item by its value from all items (including shadow items).
   137	    /// </summary>
   138	    public bool TryGetShadowItemByValue(T? value, [NotNullWhen(true)] out MudSelectItem<T>? item)
   139	    {
   140	        return _shadowLookup.TryGetValue(value, out item);
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    /// <summary>
   144	    /// Subscribes to selection changes.
   145	    /// </summary>
   146	    /// <param name="observer">The callback to invoke when selection changes.</param>
   147	    /// <returns>A disposable subscription that can be used to unsubscribe.</returns>
   148	    public IDisposable SubscribeToSelectionChanges(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   149	    {
   150	        _selectionObservers.Add(observer);
   151	        return new SelectionSubscription(this, observer);
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    /// <summary>
   155	    /// Unsubscribes an observer from selection changes.
   156	    /// </summary>
   157	    private void Unsubscribe(Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   158	    {
   159	        _selectionObservers.Remove(observer);
   160	    }
   161	
   162	    /// <summary>
   163	    /// Notifies all observers of a selection change.
   164	    /// </summary>
   165	    public async Task NotifySelectionChangedAsync()
   166	    {
   167	        var selectedValues = SelectedValues;
   168	        for (var i = _selectionObservers.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
   169	        {
   170	            await _selectionObservers[i](selectedValues);
   171	        }
   172	    }
   173	
   174	    private sealed class SelectionSubscription(MudSelectContext<T> context, Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task> observer)
   175	        : IDisposable
   176	    {
   177	        private MudSelectContext<T>? _context = context;
   178	        private Func<IReadOnlyCollection<T?>, Task>? _observer = observer;
   179	
   180	        public void Dispose()
   181	        {
   182	            var contextCopy = _context;
   183	            var observerCopy = _observer;
   184	
   185	            if (contextCopy is null || observerCopy is null)
   186	            {
   187	                return;
   188	            }
   189	
   190	            _context = null;
   191	            _observer = null;
   192	
   193	            contextCopy.Unsubscribe(observerCopy);
   194	        }
   195	    }
   196	}

     2	// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
