     5	using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;
     6	using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     7	using Microsoft.JSInterop;
     8	
     9	namespace MudBlazor;
    10	
    11	
    12	/// <summary>
    13	/// A base class for implementing Popover components.
    14	/// </summary>
    15	/// <remarks>
    16	/// This class provides a base implementation for a Popover component. It implements the <see cref="IPopover"/> interface
    17	/// and utilizes the <see cref="IPopoverService"/> to handle the creation, updating, and destruction of the popover.
    18	/// </remarks>
    19	public abstract class MudPopoverBase : MudComponentBase, IPopover, IAsyncDisposable
    20	{
    21	    private bool _afterFirstRender;
    22	
    23	    /// <inheritdoc />
    24	    public virtual Guid Id { get; } = Guid.NewGuid();
    25	
    26	    [Inject]
    27	    protected IPopoverService PopoverService { get; set; } = null!;
    28	
    29	    /// <inheritdoc />
    30	    string IPopover.PopoverClass => PopoverClass;
    31	
    32	    /// <inheritdoc />
    33	    string IPopover.PopoverStyles => PopoverStyles;
    34	
    35	    protected internal abstract string PopoverClass { get; }
    36	
    37	    protected internal abstract string PopoverStyles { get; }
    38	
    39	    /// <inheritdoc />
    40	    [Parameter]
    41	    [Category(CategoryTypes.Popover.Behavior)]
    42	    public bool Open { get; set; }
    43	
    44	    /// <inheritdoc />
    45	    [Parameter]
    46	    [Category(CategoryTypes.Popover.Behavior)]
    47	    public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    48	
    49	    /// <inheritdoc />
    50	    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    51	    {
    52	        await PopoverService.CreatePopoverAsync(this);
    53	
    54	        await base.OnInitializedAsync();
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    /// <inheritdoc />
    58	    protected override async Task OnParametersSetAsync()
    59	    {
    60	        await base.OnParametersSetAsync();
    61	
    62	        if (_afterFirstRender)
    63	        {
    64	            await PopoverService.UpdatePopoverAsync(this);
    65	        }
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    /// <inheritdoc />
    69	    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    70	    {
    71	        if (firstRender)
    72	        {
    73	            await PopoverService.UpdatePopoverAsync(this);
    74	
    75	            _afterFirstRender = true;
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    /// <inheritdoc />
    82	    [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
    83	    public virtual async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    84	    {
    85	        try
    86	        {
    87	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable)
    88	            {
    89	                await PopoverService.DestroyPopoverAsync(this);
    90	            }
    91	        }
    92	        catch (JSDisconnectedException) { }
    93	        catch (TaskCanceledException) { }
    94	    }
    95	}
     1	﻿// Copyright (c) MudBlazor 2021
     2	// MudBlazor licenses this file to you under the MIT license.
     3	// See the LICENSE file in the project root for more information.
     4	
     5	using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     6	using MudBlazor.Interfaces;
     7	
     8	namespace MudBlazor
     9	{
    10	
    11	    /// <summary>
    12	    /// A required component which manages all MudBlazor popovers.
    13	    /// </summary>
    14	    /// <remarks>
    15	    /// This component is required for MudBlazor components to display popovers properly.  It is typically added to your main layout page.
    16	    /// </remarks>
    17	    /// <seealso cref="MudThemeProvider"/>
    18	    /// <seealso cref="MudDialogProvider"/>
    19	    /// <seealso cref="MudSnackbarProvider"/>
    20	    public partial class MudPopoverProvider : IDisposable, IPopoverObserver
    21	    {
    22	        private bool _isConnectedToService;
    23	
    24	        [Inject]
    25	        internal IPopoverService PopoverService { get; set; } = null!;
    26	
    27	        /// <summary>
    28	        /// Controls whether this provider is enabled.
    29	        /// </summary>
    30	        /// <remarks>
    31	        /// Defaults to <c>true</c>.
    32	        /// If more than one <see cref="MudPopoverProvider"/> is detected, this property will be <c>false</c> to ensure only one instance is active.
    33	        /// Can be overridden by setting a cascading parameter of <c>UsePopoverProvider</c> to <c>false</c>.
    34	        /// </remarks>
    35	        [CascadingParameter(Name = "UsePopoverProvider")]
    36	        public bool Enabled { get; set; } = true;
    37	
    38	        /// <summary>
    39	        /// Releases resources used by this provider.
    40	        /// </summary>
    41	        public void Dispose()
    42	        {
    43	            PopoverService.Unsubscribe(this);
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        /// <inheritdoc />
    47	        protected override void OnInitialized()
    48	        {
    49	            if (!Enabled)
    50	            {
    51	                return;
    52	            }
    53	
    54	            PopoverService.Subscribe(this);
    55	            _isConnectedToService = true;
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        /// <inheritdoc />
    59	        protected override void OnParametersSet()
    60	        {
    61	            base.OnParametersSet();
    62	
    63	            if (!Enabled && _isConnectedToService)
    64	            {
    65	                PopoverService.Unsubscribe(this);
    66	                _isConnectedToService = false;
    67	
    68	                return;
    69	            }
    70	
    71	            // Let's in our new case ignore _isConnectedToService and always update the subscription except Enabled = false. The manager is specifically designed for it.
    72	            // The reason is because If an observer throws an exception during the PopoverCollectionUpdatedNotification, indicating a malfunction, it will be automatically unsubscribed.
    73	            if (Enabled)
    74	            {
    75	                PopoverService.Subscribe(this);
    76	            }
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        /// <inheritdoc />
    80	        protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    81	        {
    82	            if (firstRender && Enabled && PopoverService.PopoverOptions.ThrowOnDuplicateProvider)
    83	            {
    84	                if (await PopoverService.GetProviderCountAsync() > 1)
    85	                {
    86	                    throw new InvalidOperationException("Duplicate MudPopoverProvider detected. Please ensure there is only one provider, or disable this warning with PopoverOptions.ThrowOnDuplicateProvider.");
    87	                }
    88	            }
    89	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        /// <inheritdoc />
    93	        Guid IPopoverObserver.Id { get; } = Guid.NewGuid();
    94	
    95	        /// <inheritdoc />
    96	        async Task IPopoverObserver.PopoverCollectionUpdatedNotificationAsync(PopoverHolderContainer container, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
    97	        {
    98	            switch (container.Operation)
    99	            {
   100	                // Update popover individually
   101	                case PopoverHolderOperation.Update:
   102	                    {
   103	                        foreach (var holder in container.Holders)
   104	                        {
   105	                            if (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)
   106	                            {
   107	                                return;
   108	                            }
   109	
   110	                            if (holder.ElementReference is IMudStateHasChanged stateHasChanged)
   111	                            {
   112	                                await InvokeAsync(stateHasChanged.StateHasChanged);
   113	                            }
   114	                        }
   115	
   116	                        break;
   117	                    }
   118	                // Update whole MudPopoverProvider
   119	                case PopoverHolderOperation.Create:
   120	                case PopoverHolderOperation.Remove:
   121	                    await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   122	                    break;
   123	            }
   124	        }
   125	    }
   126	}
     1	﻿@namespace MudBlazor
     2	
     3	@if (Enabled)
     4	{
     5	    <div class="@PopoverService.PopoverOptions.ContainerClass">
     6	        <SectionOutlet SectionName="mud-overlay-to-popover-provider" />
     7	        @foreach (var handler in PopoverService.ActivePopovers)
     8	        {
     9	            <MudRender @ref="handler.ElementReference" @key="handler.Id">
    10	                <div id="@($"popovercontent-{handler.Id}")" data-ticks="@(handler.ActivationDate?.Ticks ?? 0)" @attributes="@handler.UserAttributes" class="@handler.Class" style="@handler.Style">
    11	                    @if (handler.ShowContent)
    12	                    {
    13	                        @handler.Fragment
    14	                    }
    15	                </div>
    16	            </MudRender>
    17	        }
    18	    </div>
    19	}

    10	    /// <summary>
    11	    /// A scrollable list for displaying text, avatars, and icons. Use lists to help users find a specific item and act on it.
    12	    /// </summary>
    13	    /// <remarks>
    14	    /// This component contains an optional <see cref="MudListSubheader"/> and one or more <see cref="MudListItem{T}"/>.
    15	    /// </remarks>
    16	    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of item being listed.</typeparam>
    17	    /// <seealso cref="MudListItem{T}"/>
    18	    /// <seealso cref="MudListSubheader"/>
    19	    public partial class MudList<T> : MudComponentBase, IDisposable
    20	    {
    21	        public MudList()
    22	        {
    23	            TopLevelList = this;
    24	            using var registerScope = CreateRegisterScope();
    25	            _selectedValueState = registerScope.RegisterParameter<T?>(nameof(SelectedValue))
    26	                .WithParameter(() => SelectedValue)
    27	                .WithEventCallback(() => SelectedValueChanged)
    28	                .WithChangeHandler(OnSelectedValueParameterChangedAsync)
    29	                .WithComparer(() => Comparer);
    30	            _selectedValuesState = registerScope.RegisterParameter<IReadOnlyCollection<T>?>(nameof(SelectedValues))
    31	                .WithParameter(() => SelectedValues)
    32	                .WithEventCallback(() => SelectedValuesChanged)
    33	                .WithChangeHandler(OnSelectedValuesChangedAsync)
    34	                .WithComparer(() => Comparer, x => new CollectionComparer<T>(x));
    35	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<IEqualityComparer<T?>>(nameof(Comparer))
    36	                .WithParameter(() => Comparer)
    37	                .WithChangeHandler(OnComparerChangedAsync);
    38	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<SelectionMode>(nameof(SelectionMode))
    39	                .WithParameter(() => SelectionMode)
    40	                .WithChangeHandler(UpdateSelection);
    41	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(Dense))
    42	                .WithParameter(() => Dense)
    43	                .WithChangeHandler(Update);
    44	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(Disabled))
    45	                .WithParameter(() => Disabled)
    46	                .WithChangeHandler(Update);
    47	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(ReadOnly))
    48	                .WithParameter(() => ReadOnly)
    49	                .WithChangeHandler(Update);
    50	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<bool>(nameof(Gutters))
    51	                .WithParameter(() => Gutters)
    52	                .WithChangeHandler(Update);
    53	        }

cat > /tmp/repro_select_scroll.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
# Reproduce the lifecycle bug in MudSelect.OpenMenu(): it scrolls synchronously
# before visible MudSelectItems register after the render. In the source this is
# represented by _needsHighlightAfterRender handling in OnAfterRenderAsync not
# performing any scroll after HighlightItemForValueAsync.
file="src/MudBlazor/Components/Select/MudSelect.razor.cs"
open_scroll=$(awk '/public async Task OpenMenu\(\)/,/KeyInterceptorService.UpdateKeyAsync/' "$file" | grep -c 'ScrollToItemAsync(item)' || true)
after_render_block=$(awk '/if \(_needsHighlightAfterRender\)/,/^            }/' "$file")
after_render_scroll=$(printf '%s\n' "$after_render_block" | grep -c 'ScrollToItemAsync\|ScrollToSelected' || true)
if [ "$open_scroll" -gt 0 ] && [ "$after_render_scroll" -eq 0 ]; then
  echo "FAIL: OpenMenu scrolls before post-render item registration, and post-render highlight does not scroll."
  exit 1
fi
echo "PASS: selected item scroll is deferred until after items are rendered."
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_select_scroll.sh
/tmp/repro_select_scroll.sh
